(u'https://farm1.staticflickr.com/753/22182117233_3a2d948092.jpg', {'description': u'<a href="http://www.danielnovakphoto.com/" rel="nofollow">\xa9 2015 Daniel Novak Photo</a> | <a href="http://www.danielnovakphoto.com/blog" rel="nofollow">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/danielnovakphot/" rel="nofollow">Pinterest</a> | <a href="https://instagram.com/danielnovakphoto/" rel="nofollow">Instagram</a>\n\n<b>\xa9 All rights reserved!</b>\n\nOne of a dozen of new matted and signed arrivals to Picture Your Walls Western New York ...\n\n<a href="http://www.danielnovakphoto.com/blog/2015/10/new-arrivals-of-daniel-novak-photo-in-picture-your-walls" rel="nofollow">New Arrivals of Daniel Novak Photo in Picture Your Walls</a>\n\n... The final photo in this series was not too far. As I continued my morning hike I walked through the beautiful tree tunnels I enjoy a lot and have photographed many times. I tried a few new approaches but did not like any of the images more than the previous ones so out to trash they went.\n\nHowever, when I faced the leaning trees with their dark trunks visually accentuating the colorful foliage of theirs I could not resist. It seemed like the perfect exclamation mark after a great morning outdoors. It helped me capture the different moods of the park on a single fall rainy morning, with areas of only subtle colors, some areas already bare, and some screaming fall at full blast.\n\nI really liked that ...\n\n<a href="http://www.danielnovakphoto.com/blog/2014/10/the-fall-concert-at-birdsong" rel="nofollow">The Fall Concert at Birdsong</a>', 'comments': [u'Really good warm colours to look good on someones wall.', u'Thanks [https://www.flickr.com/photos/27955898@N07]!', u'awesome', u'Beautiful image, Dan', u'Nice tones and colors', u'Amazing fall scene!', u'Nice, I love the contrast on this one.\n~ Commented with <a href="http://flickrstudioapp.com" rel="nofollow">Flickr Studio</a> for iPad.', u'Amazing colors and framing!'], 'title': u'The Music of Fall at Birdsong - Matted & Signed at PYWWNY, Hamburg, NY (DTB_4896)'})
